Method: 研究采用共享任务设计，提出叙事相似性的二元分类范式：给定锚点故事和两个候选故事，判断哪个更相似。方法包括：(1) 构建新型叙事相似性定义，融合叙事理论与直觉判断；(2) 采集超过1000个故事摘要三元组，每个标注由至少两名标注者一致确认；(3) 设立两条赛道：三元组分类任务和嵌入表征评估任务；(4) 分析71个提交系统的技术特点，对比LLM集成、预训练模型前后处理与定制微调方案的性能差异。

Result: 数据集包含至少2000个高质量标注（1000+三元组×2个标注），覆盖两条任务赛道。参赛系统显示：三元组分类任务中，LLM集成方法占据主导地位，成为顶尖系统的核心技术；嵌入任务中，对预训练嵌入模型进行前后处理的方法性能与定制化微调方案相当，差距微乎其微。分析表明，现有自动化系统在叙事相似性建模方面仍存在明显提升空间。任务网站提供了所有团队的嵌入可视化及实例级分类结果。

Conclusion: NSNRL任务成功建立了首个融合叙事理论与直觉的标准化评估体系，验证了LLM在叙事理解上的潜力，同时揭示了预训练模型通过适当前后处理即可达到良好效果，降低了技术门槛。研究为叙事表征学习提供了基准数据集和性能基线，指出未来方向需进一步缩小自动化系统与人类判断之间的差距，提升模型在深层叙事结构和语义理解上的能力。

Abstract: We present the shared task on narrative similarity and narrative representation learning - NSNRL (pronounced "nass-na-rel"). The task operationalizes narrative similarity as a binary classification problem: determining which of two stories is more similar to an anchor story. We introduce a novel definition of narrative similarity, compatible with both narrative theory and intuitive judgment. Based on the similarity judgments collected under this concept, we also evaluate narrative embedding representations. We collected at least two annotations each for more than 1,000 story summary triples, with each annotation being backed by at least two annotators in agreement. This paper describes the sampling and annotation process for the dataset; further, we give an overview of the submitted systems and the techniques they employ. We received a total of 71 final submissions from 46 teams across our two tracks. In our triple-based classification setup, LLM ensembles make up many of the top-scoring systems, while in the embedding setup, systems with pre- and post-processing on pretrained embedding models perform about on par with custom fine-tuned solutions. Our analysis identifies potential headroom for improvement of automated systems in both tracks. The task website includes visualizations of embeddings alongside instance-level classification results for all teams.

### [48] [Machine Behavior in Relational Moral Dilemmas: Moral Rightness, Predicted Human Behavior, and Model Decisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21871)
*Jiseon Kim,Jea Kwon,Luiz Felipe Vecchietti,Wenchao Dong,Jaehong Kim,Meeyoung Cha*

TL;DR: 本研究通过"吹哨人困境"框架检验大语言模型是否编码了情境依赖的道德判断。研究发现，尽管模型能预测人类行为随关系亲密而转向忠诚，但其自身决策却始终遵循公平导向的道德规则，二者存在显著分歧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型日益成为决策支持系统，确定它们是否能够捕捉人类道德判断中依赖情境和人际关系的社会细微差别至关重要。

Method: 采用"吹哨人困境"范式，操纵犯罪严重性和关系亲密度两个维度，从道德正确性（规范准则）、预测人类行为（描述性社会期望）和模型自主决策三个视角评估，并分析其推理过程。

Result: 发现明显的跨视角分歧：道德正确性判断始终偏向公平；预测人类行为随关系亲密显著转向忠诚；而模型决策与其道德判断一致，而非其自身的行为预测。

Conclusion: 大语言模型的决策优先考虑僵化的规范规则，而非其内部世界建模中所体现的社会敏感性，这种不一致性可能在真实部署中导致严重的对齐问题。

Abstract: Human moral judgment is context-dependent and modulated by interpersonal relationships. As large language models (LLMs) increasingly function as decision-support systems, determining whether they encode these social nuances is critical. We characterize machine behavior using the Whistleblower's Dilemma by varying two experimental dimensions: crime severity and relational closeness. Our study evaluates three distinct perspectives: (1) moral rightness (prescriptive norms), (2) predicted human behavior (descriptive social expectations), and (3) autonomous model decision-making. By analyzing the reasoning processes, we identify a clear cross-perspective divergence: while moral rightness remains consistently fairness-oriented, predicted human behavior shifts significantly toward loyalty as relational closeness increases. Crucially, model decisions align with moral rightness judgments rather than their own behavioral predictions. This inconsistency suggests that LLM decision-making prioritizes rigid, prescriptive rules over the social sensitivity present in their internal world-modeling, which poses a gap that may lead to significant misalignments in real-world deployments.

</details>


### [49] [Revisiting Non-Verbatim Memorization in Large Language Models: The Role of Entity Surface Forms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21882)
*Yuto Nishida,Naoki Shikoda,Yosuke Kishinami,Ryo Fujii,Makoto Morishita,Hidetaka Kamigaito,Taro Watanabe*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过RedirectQA数据集发现，大语言模型的事实记忆对实体表层形式的依赖性具有类别特异性，既非完全表面特定也非完全表面不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解大语言模型记忆的事实知识类型对于评估其可靠性至关重要。现有基于实体的问答评估通常使用单一标准表层形式，难以区分模型是真正记忆了事实还是仅通过特定名称访问知识。

Method: 提出RedirectQA数据集，利用维基百科重定向信息将Wikidata事实三元组与多种实体表层形式（别名、缩写、拼写变体及错误形式）关联，并在13个大语言模型上检验表层形式条件化的事实记忆。

Result: 实验发现仅改变实体表层形式即可改变预测结果，且这种不一致性具有类别依赖性：模型对细微正字法变体的鲁棒性高于对别名和缩写等较大词汇变化的鲁棒性。频率分析表明实体和表层频率均与准确率相关，实体频率的贡献超越表层频率。

Conclusion: 事实记忆既非纯表层特定也非完全表层不变，强调了在评估非字面记忆时表层形式多样性的重要性。

Abstract: Understanding what kinds of factual knowledge large language models (LLMs) memorize is essential for evaluating their reliability and limitations. Entity-based QA is a common framework for analyzing non-verbatim memorization, but typical evaluations query each entity using a single canonical surface form, making it difficult to disentangle fact memorization from access through a particular name. We introduce RedirectQA, an entity-based QA dataset that uses Wikipedia redirect information to associate Wikidata factual triples with categorized surface forms for each entity, including alternative names, abbreviations, spelling variants, and common erroneous forms. Across 13 LLMs, we examine surface-conditioned factual memorization and find that prediction outcomes often change when only the entity surface form changes. This inconsistency is category-dependent: models are more robust to minor orthographic variations than to larger lexical variations such as aliases and abbreviations. Frequency analyses further suggest that both entity- and surface-level frequencies are associated with accuracy, and that entity frequency often contributes beyond surface frequency. Overall, factual memorization appears neither purely surface-specific nor fully surface-invariant, highlighting the importance of surface-form diversity in evaluating non-verbatim memorization.

</details>


### [50] [A Multimodal Text- and Graph-Based Approach for Open-Domain Event Extraction from Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21885)
*Praval Sharma*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前事件抽取面临双重挑战：封闭域方法局限于预定义事件类型，泛化能力差；开放域方法虽能处理任意事件类型，但未能充分利用大型语言模型的强大能力，且缺乏对文档级上下文、结构和语义推理的显式建模。这些推理对 LLM 至关重要但充满挑战，易受"中间丢失"现象和注意力稀释问题影响。

Method: 提出 MODEE 框架，创新性地将图学习与 LLM 文本表示相结合。通过图结构显式建模文档内部的深层语义关系和推理路径，同时利用 LLM 捕捉文本的上下文语义，从而实现对文档级上下文、结构和语义推理的联合建模，克服 LLM 在长文档处理中的局限性。

Result: 在大规模数据集上的实验表明，MODEE 在开放域事件抽取上显著优于现有最优方法，同时具备向封闭域任务迁移的能力，在该领域同样超越现有算法，验证了其有效性和泛化性。

Conclusion: MODEE 通过融合图结构与 LLM 表示，成功解决了开放域事件抽取中的文档级推理挑战，不仅性能卓越，还展现了强大的跨域泛化能力，为事件抽取研究提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Event extraction is essential for event understanding and analysis. It supports tasks such as document summarization and decision-making in emergency scenarios. However, existing event extraction approaches have limitations: (1) closed-domain algorithms are restricted to predefined event types and thus rarely generalize to unseen types and (2) open-domain event extraction algorithms, capable of handling unconstrained event types, have largely overlooked the potential of large language models (LLMs) despite their advanced abilities. Additionally, they do not explicitly model document-level contextual, structural, and semantic reasoning, which are crucial for effective event extraction but remain challenging for LLMs due to lost-in-the-middle phenomenon and attention dilution. To address these limitations, we propose multimodal open-domain event extraction, MODEE , a novel approach for open-domain event extraction that combines graph-based learning with text-based representation from LLMs to model document-level reasoning. Empirical evaluations on large datasets demonstrate that MODEE outperforms state-of-the-art open-domain event extraction approaches and can be generalized to closed-domain event extraction, where it outperforms existing algorithms.

  <summary>Details</summary>

In this paper, we present TingIS, an end-to-end system designed for enterprise-grade incident discovery. At the core of TingIS is a multi-stage event linking engine that synergizes efficient indexing techniques with Large Language Models (LLMs) to make informed decisions on event merging, enabling the stable extraction of actionable incidents from just a handful of diverse user descriptions. This engine is complemented by a cascaded routing mechanism for precise business attribution and a multi-dimensional noise reduction pipeline that integrates domain knowledge, statistical patterns, and behavioral filtering. Deployed in a production environment handling a peak throughput of over 2,000 messages per minute and 300,000 messages per day, TingIS achieves a P90 alert latency of 3.5 minutes and a 95\% discovery rate for high-priority incidents. Benchmarks constructed from real-world data demonstrate that TingIS significantly outperforms baseline methods in routing accuracy, clustering quality, and Signal-to-Noise Ratio.

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出结合历时文体分析、语境主题建模和语义聚类的可扩展计算框架，对巴西国会2003-2025年45万篇演讲进行大规模分析，揭示演讲风格趋向简短直接、立法议程随国家危机剧烈转向，以及话语联盟中地域和性别身份比党派归属更具区分度的现象，为议会话语分析提供了补充传统投票研究的新方法。

Abstract: Analyses of legislative behavior often rely on voting records, overlooking the rich semantic and rhetorical content of political speech. In this paper, we ask three complementary questions about parliamentary discourse: how things are said, what is being said, and who is speaking in discursively similar ways. To answer these questions, we introduce a scalable and generalizable computational framework that combines diachronic stylometric analysis, contextual topic modeling, and semantic clustering of deputies' speeches. We apply this framework to a large-scale case study of the Brazilian Chamber of Deputies, using a corpus of over 450,000 speeches from 2003 to 2025. Our results show a long-term stylistic shift toward shorter and more direct speeches, a legislative agenda that reorients sharply in response to national crises, and a granular map of discursive alignments in which regional and gender identities often prove more salient than formal party affiliation. More broadly, this work offers a robust methodology for analyzing parliamentary discourse as a multidimensional phenomenon that complements traditional vote-based approaches.

### [54] [GiVA: Gradient-Informed Bases for Vector-Based Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21901)
*Neeraj Gangwar,Rishabh Deshmukh,Michael Shavlovsky,Hancao Li,Vivek Mittal,Lexing Ying,Nickvash Kani*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GiVA是一种用于向量适应的基于梯度的初始化策略，它通过8倍的秩缩减，在保持极高参数效率的同时，实现了与LoRA相当的训练速度和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着模型规模持续增大，全量微调成本高昂，参数高效微调成为重要替代方案。尽管LoRA被广泛采用，但向量适应方法因具有极高的参数效率而受到关注。然而，这些方法通常需要比LoRA高得多的秩才能达到相当性能，导致训练成本增加。

Method: 提出GiVA，一种基于梯度的向量适应初始化策略。该方法通过智能初始化来降低对高秩的需求，同时保持向量适应的极端参数效率优势，并实现与LoRA相当的训练时间。

Conclusion: GiVA成功解决了向量适应方法需要高秩的问题，通过梯度初始化策略实现了参数效率与训练效率的平衡，为大规模模型的高效微调提供了新方案。

This work introduces GiVA, a gradient-based initialization strategy for vector-based adaptation. It achieves training times comparable to LoRA and maintains the extreme parameter efficiency of vector-based adaptation. We evaluate GiVA across diverse benchmarks, including natural language understanding, natural language generation, and image classification. ### [55] [MathDuels: Evaluating LLMs as Problem Posers and Solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21916)
*Zhiqiu Xu,Shibo Jin,Shreya Arya,Mayur Naik*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对静态数学基准测试天花板效应，提出MathDuels自博弈评估框架，通过模型间对抗出题与解题，结合Rasch模型联合评估，揭示隐藏的能力差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿语言模型在静态数学基准上性能接近饱和，现有评估方法无法有效区分模型能力，且仅评估单角色求解能力，忽略了问题生成这一重要维度。

Method: 构建双角色自博弈系统：1) 三阶段问题生成管道（元提示→问题生成→难度放大）；2) 独立验证器过滤无效问题；3) 采用Rasch模型联合估计解题者能力和问题难度，以作者生成问题的难度衡量其质量。

Result: 在19个模型上的实验发现：出题与解题能力部分解耦；双角色评估揭示了单角色测试无法识别的能力分化；新模型生成的题目能击败旧模型，实现基准难度与模型能力的协同进化，避免性能饱和。

Conclusion: MathDuels建立了动态演化的评估新范式，提供了持续区分模型能力的有效工具，并通过公开排行榜推动社区发展。

Abstract: As frontier language models attain near-ceiling performance on static mathematical benchmarks, existing evaluations are increasingly unable to differentiate model capabilities, largely because they cast models solely as solvers of fixed problem sets. We introduce MathDuels, a self-play benchmark in which models occupy dual roles: each authors math problems under adversarial prompting and solves problems authored by every other participant. Problems are produced through a three-stage generation pipeline (meta-prompting, problem generation, and difficulty amplification), and validated by an independent verifier that excludes ill-posed questions. A Rasch model (Rasch, 1993) jointly estimates solver abilities and problem difficulties; author quality is derived from the difficulties of each model's authored problems. Experiments across 19 frontier models reveal that authoring and solving capabilities are partially decoupled, and that dual-role evaluation reveals capability separations invisible in single-role benchmarks. As newer models enter the arena, they produce problems that defeat previously dominant solvers, so the benchmark's difficulty co-evolves with participant strength rather than saturating at a fixed ceiling. We host a public leaderboard that updates as new models are released.

</details>


### [56] [Evaluation of Automatic Speech Recognition Using Generative Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21928)
*Thibault Bañeras-Roux,Shashi Kumar,Driss Khalil,Sergio Burdisso,Petr Motlicek,Shiran Liu,Mickael Rouvier,Jane Wottawa,Richard Dufour*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探索了解码器架构大语言模型在自动语音识别语义评估中的应用，提出三种评估范式，在HATS数据集上实现92-94%人类标注一致性，显著超越传统词错误率指标，展现了LLM在可解释语义评估中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统词错误率（WER）指标无法捕捉识别结果的语义保真度，而现有嵌入式语义指标虽与人工评价相关性更佳，但基于解码器的大语言模型在该领域的应用尚未得到充分探索，存在研究空白。

Method: 采用三种评估范式：（1）二元假设选择，判断两个候选识别结果中哪个更优；（2）生成式嵌入语义距离计算，量化识别结果与参考答案的语义差异；（3）错误定性分类，对识别错误进行语义层面的类型划分。

Result: 在HATS数据集上，最优LLM的假设选择准确率达92-94%，远超WER的63%一致性；解码器LLM的嵌入表示性能与编码器模型相当；LLM在各类语义评估指标上均优于传统方法。

Conclusion: 解码器大语言模型为可解释、语义敏感的语音识别评估提供了新方向，其评估结果与人类感知高度对齐，具有广泛应用前景。

Abstract: Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) is traditionally evaluated using Word Error Rate (WER), a metric that is insensitive to meaning. Embedding-based semantic metrics are better correlated with human perception, but decoder-based Large Language Models (LLMs) remain underexplored for this task. This paper evaluates their relevance through three approaches: (1) selecting the best hypothesis between two candidates, (2) computing semantic distance using generative embeddings, and (3) qualitative classification of errors. On the HATS dataset, the best LLMs achieve 92--94\% agreement with human annotators for hypothesis selection, compared to 63\% for WER, also outperforming semantic metrics. Embeddings from decoder-based LLMs show performance comparable to encoder models. Finally, LLMs offer a promising direction for interpretable and semantic ASR evaluation.

</details>

### [57] [AtomicRAG: Atom-Entity Graphs for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20844)
*Yanning Hou,Duanyang Yuan,Sihang Zhou,Xiaoshu Chen,Ke Liang,Siwei Wang,Xinwang Liu,Jian Huang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文针对现有GraphRAG方法中文本块表示僵化和三元组实体链接易出错的问题，提出Atom-Entity图和AtomicRAG算法，使用知识原子实现灵活的知识重组，结合个性化PageRank与相关性过滤提高推理可靠性，在五个基准测试中超越现有RAG基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GraphRAG方法以文本块为基本单位，导致多个原子事实被刚性捆绑，限制了应对多样化检索场景的灵活性和适应性；同时基于三元组的实体链接对关系抽取错误敏感，易产生错误推理路径。因此需要更精确可靠的知识表示与索引架构。

Method: 提出Atom-Entity图架构，将知识存储为独立、自包含的知识原子而非粗粒度文本块；实体间边仅表示关系存在与否；结合个性化PageRank与基于相关性的过滤机制维护准确的实体连接，构建AtomicRAG算法。

Result: 在五个公开基准测试上的理论分析和实验表明，AtomicRAG在检索准确性和推理鲁棒性方面优于现有强RAG基线。

Conclusion: Atom-Entity图通过原子化知识表示和简化的实体连接机制，实现了更灵活、精确和可靠的知识检索与推理，为RAG系统提供了新的架构范式。

Abstract: Recent GraphRAG methods integrate graph structures into text indexing and retrieval, using knowledge graph triples to connect text chunks, thereby improving retrieval coverage and precision. However, we observe that treating text chunks as the basic unit of knowledge representation rigidly groups multiple atomic facts together, limiting the flexibility and adaptability needed to support diverse retrieval scenarios. Additionally, triple-based entity linking is sensitive to relation-extraction errors, which can lead to missing or incorrect reasoning paths and ultimately hurt retrieval accuracy. To address these issues, we propose the Atom-Entity Graph, a more precise and reliable architecture for knowledge representation and indexing. In our approach, knowledge is stored as knowledge atoms, namely individual, self-contained units of factual information, rather than coarse-grained text chunks. This allows knowledge elements to be flexibly reassembled without mutual interference, thereby enabling seamless alignment with diverse query perspectives. Edges between entities simply indicate whether a relationship exists. By combining personalized PageRank with relevance-based filtering, we maintain accurate entity connections and improve the reliability of reasoning. Theoretical analysis and experiments on five public benchmarks show that the proposed AtomicRAG algorithm outperforms strong RAG baselines in retrieval accuracy and reasoning robustness. Code: https://github.com/7HHHHH/AtomicRAG.

</details>


### [58] [ADS-POI: Agentic Spatiotemporal State Decomposition for Next Point-of-Interest Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20846)
*Zhenyu Yu,Chunlei Meng,Yangchen Zeng,Mohd Yamani Idna Idris,Shuigeng Zhou*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出ADS-POI框架，通过将用户历史行为分解为多个具有不同时空动态的并行潜在子状态来解决下一个兴趣点推荐中的异质性信号纠缠问题，这些子状态通过上下文条件机制选择性聚合，从而在多个真实世界数据集上实现更优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将用户历史压缩为单一潜在表示，导致常规移动模式、短期意图和时间规律等异质信号相互纠缠，限制了状态演化的灵活性，降低了模型适应多样决策上下文的能力。

Method: ADS-POI采用时空状态分解框架，将用户表示为多个并行演化的潜在子状态，每个子状态受独立的时空转移动力学控制；通过上下文条件聚合机制动态组合这些子状态形成预测用的决策状态。

Result: 在Foursquare和Gowalla三个真实基准数据集上的广泛实验表明，ADS-POI在全排序评估协议下持续优于现有强基线方法，验证了多状态分解的有效性。

Conclusion: 将用户行为分解为多个时空感知状态能实现不同行为组件以不同速率协同演化，从而产生更有效、更鲁棒的下一个兴趣点推荐效果。

Abstract: Next point-of-interest (POI) recommendation requires modeling user mobility as a spatiotemporal sequence, where different behavioral factors may evolve at different temporal and spatial scales. Most existing methods compress a user's history into a single latent representation, which tends to entangle heterogeneous signals such as routine mobility patterns, short-term intent, and temporal regularities. This entanglement limits the flexibility of state evolution and reduces the model's ability to adapt to diverse decision contexts. We propose ADS-POI, a spatiotemporal state decomposition framework for next POI recommendation. ADS-POI represents a user with multiple parallel evolving latent sub-states, each governed by its own spatiotemporal transition dynamics. These sub-states are selectively aggregated through a context-conditioned mechanism to form the decision state used for prediction. This design enables different behavioral components to evolve at different rates while remaining coordinated under the current spatiotemporal context. Extensive experiments on three real-world benchmark datasets from Foursquare and Gowalla demonstrate that ADS-POI consistently outperforms strong state-of-the-art baselines under a full-ranking evaluation protocol. The results show that decomposing user behavior into multiple spatiotemporally aware states leads to more effective and robust next POI recommendation. Our code is available at https://github.com/YuZhenyuLindy/ADS-POI.git.

</details>

Method: 构建TASTE数据集，集成音频和文本双模态信息；利用大规模自监督音乐编码器提取音频表征；提出MuQ-token方法，通过智能聚合策略实现多层音频特征的高效整合，替代传统简单的平均或拼接方式。

Result: 实验表明，所提取的音频表征在候选召回和点击率预测任务中均带来显著性能提升；MuQ-token方法在不同实验设置下持续优于其他特征融合技术，验证了多模态信息特别是音频内容在推荐任务中的价值。

Conclusion: 研究证实了内容驱动方法在音乐推荐中的有效性，TASTE为学术界提供了高质量的多模态数据集和基准框架，MuQ-token为特征融合提供了新思路，将推动冷启动推荐、多模态学习等相关领域的研究进展。

Abstract: Music Recommendation Systems (MRSs) are a cornerstone of modern streaming platforms. Existing recommendation models, spanning both recall and ranking stages, predominantly rely on collaborative filtering, which fails to exploit the intrinsic characteristics of audio and consequently leads to suboptimal performance, particularly in cold-start scenarios. However, existing music recommendation datasets often lack rich multimodal information, such as raw audio signals and descriptive textual metadata. Moreover, current recommender system evaluation frameworks remain inadequate, as they neither fully leverage multimodal information nor support a diverse range of algorithms, especially multimodal methods. To address these limitations, we propose TASTE, a comprehensive dataset and benchmarking framework designed to highlight the role of multimodal information in music recommendation. Our dataset integrates both audio and textual modalities. By leveraging recent large-scale self-supervised music encoders, we demonstrate the substantial value of the extracted audio representations across recommendation tasks, including candidate recall and CTR. In addition, we introduce the \textbf{MuQ-token} method, which enables more efficient integration of multi-layer audio features. This method consistently outperforms other feature integration techniques across various settings. Overall, our results not only validate the effectiveness of content-driven approaches but also provide a highly effective and reusable multimodal foundation for future research. Code is available at https://github.com/zreach/TASTE

### [60] [MATRAG: Multi-Agent Transparent Retrieval-Augmented Generation for Explainable Recommendations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20848)
*Sushant Mehta*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM推荐系统存在透明度不足、知识 grounding 薄弱、解释性差等关键挑战，影响用户信任。用户需要可解释、可信的推荐系统来理解推荐逻辑。

Method: 提出MATRAG框架，结合多智能体协作与知识图谱增强检索。设计四个专用智能体：用户建模智能体构建动态偏好画像、项目分析智能体从知识图谱提取语义特征、推理智能体融合协同与内容信号、解释智能体生成基于检索知识的自然语言解释。引入透明度评分机制量化解释的忠实度与相关性。

Conclusion: MATRAG为透明化智能推荐系统设立了新基准，证明多智能体框架结合知识图谱检索能有效提升推荐性能与解释可信度，为生产环境部署LLM推荐器提供了可行方案与实践洞见。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based recommendation systems have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in understanding user preferences and generating personalized suggestions. However, existing approaches face critical challenges in transparency, knowledge grounding, and the ability to provide coherent explanations that foster user trust. We introduce MATRAG (Multi-Agent Transparent Retrieval-Augmented Generation), a novel framework that combined multi-agent collaboration with knowledge graph-augmented retrieval to deliver explainable recommendations. MATRAG employs four specialized agents: a User Modeling Agent that constructs dynamic preference profiles, an Item Analysis Agent that extracts semantic features from knowledge graphs, a Reasoning Agent that synthesizes collaborative and content-based signals, and an Explanation Agent that generates natural language justifications grounded in retrieved knowledge. Our framework incorporates a transparency scoring mechanism that quantifies explanation faithfulness and relevance. Extensive experiments on three benchmark datasets (Amazon Reviews, MovieLens-1M, and Yelp) demonstrate that MATRAG achieves state-of-the-art performance, improving recommendation accuracy by 12.7\% (Hit Rate) and 15.3\% (NDCG) over leading baselines, while human evaluation confirms that 87.4\% of generated explanations are rated as helpful and trustworthy by domain experts. Our work establishes new benchmarks for transparent, agentic recommendation systems and provides actionable insights for deploying LLM-based recommenders in production environments.

### [61] [SPIRE: Structure-Preserving Interpretable Retrieval of Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20849)
*Mike Rainey,Umut Acar,Muhammed Sezer*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对半结构化文档检索中结构信息丢失的问题，本文提出一种结构感知的检索流水线，通过子文档表示和双重上下文机制，在保持可扩展性的同时提升引用的质量与多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前检索增强生成技术处理HTML等半结构化数据时，因嵌入模型和生成模型的扁平序列接口与文档树形结构不匹配，导致线性化分块丢失章节、列表、表格等结构信息，难以提供既精确又可解释的小粒度引用证据。

Method: 提出结构感知检索框架：定义路径、路径集和剪枝提取等文档原语；引入全局上下文化（添加标题、列表结构等非局部框架）和局部上下文化（在结构邻域内按预算扩展）双机制；构建基于嵌入的句子种子子文档索引；设计查询时文档感知聚合策略以共享结构上下文；实施基于局部上下文视图的候选重排序过滤阶段。

Result: 在HTML问答基准测试中，该方法相比传统段落基线，在固定预算下产生质量更高、多样性更丰富的引用，同时保持了系统的可扩展性。

Conclusion: 通过保留文档结构并智能上下文化选择内容，该结构感知检索方法有效解决了半结构化数据检索的核心挑战，显著提升了小粒度证据的可解释性和可用性，且不牺牲系统效率。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation over semi-structured sources such as HTML is constrained by a mismatch between document structure and the flat, sequence-based interfaces of today's embedding and generative models. Retrieval pipelines often linearize documents into fixed-size chunks before indexing, which obscures section structure, lists, and tables, and makes it difficult to return small, citation-ready evidence without losing the surrounding context that makes it interpretable.
  We present a structure-aware retrieval pipeline that operates over tree-structured documents. The core idea is to represent candidates as subdocuments: precise, addressable selections that preserve structural identity while deferring the choice of surrounding context. We define a small set of document primitives--paths and path sets, subdocument extraction by pruning, and two contextualization mechanisms. Global contextualization adds the non-local scaffolding needed to make a selection intelligible (e.g., titles, headers, list and table structure). Local contextualization expands a seed selection within its structural neighborhood to obtain a compact, context-rich view under a target budget. Building on these primitives, we describe an embedding-based candidate generator that indexes sentence-seeded subdocuments and a query-time, document-aware aggregation step that amortizes shared structural context. We then introduce a contextual filtering stage that re-scores retrieved candidates using locally contextualized views.
  Across experiments on HTML question-answering benchmarks, we find that preserving structure while contextualizing selections yields higher-quality, more diverse citations under fixed budgets than strong passage-based baselines, while maintaining scalability.

### [62] [Association Is Not Similarity: Learning Corpus-Specific Associations for Multi-Hop Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20850)
*Jason Dury*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出Association-Augmented Retrieval (AAR)，一种轻量级转导式重排序方法。通过小型MLP（4.2M参数）和对比学习，在嵌入空间学习文档关联关系，有效提升多跳问答检索性能，无需评估集调优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稠密检索系统依赖查询与文档的嵌入相似度排序，但多跳问题需要文档间通过推理链产生的关联性。现有方法难以建模这种关联关系，导致检索性能受限。

Method: 提出AAR方法，使用小型MLP（4.2M参数）通过对比学习在共现标注上学习文档间的关联关系。推理时采用双向关联评分对稠密检索候选集进行转导式重排序。

Result: HotpotQA上Recall@5从0.831提升至0.916（+8.6点），难题提升达+28.5点；MuSiQue转导设置下提升+10.1点。归纳设置无显著改进，表明学习到的是语料库特定共现而非可迁移模式。消融实验：在语义相似但非关联对上训练性能降至基线以下，打乱关联对导致严重退化。下游QA精确匹配提升+6.4点。单查询耗时仅增3.7ms，单GPU训练不足2分钟，无需LLM索引。

Conclusion: AAR通过显式建模文档关联性显著提升多跳问答检索性能，尤其在难题上效果突出。但其转导特性限制了泛化能力，表明学习到的模式主要是语料库特定的共现关系。方法高效轻量，具有实用部署价值。

Abstract: Dense retrieval systems rank passages by embedding similarity to a query, but multi-hop questions require passages that are associatively related through shared reasoning chains. We introduce Association-Augmented Retrieval (AAR), a lightweight transductive reranking method that trains a small MLP (4.2M parameters) to learn associative relationships between passages in embedding space using contrastive learning on co-occurrence annotations. At inference time, AAR reranks an initial dense retrieval candidate set using bi-directional association scoring. On HotpotQA, AAR improves passage Recall@5 from 0.831 to 0.916 (+8.6 points) without evaluation-set tuning, with gains concentrated on hard questions where the dense baseline fails (+28.5 points). On MuSiQue, AAR achieves +10.1 points in the transductive setting. An inductive model trained on training-split associations and evaluated on unseen validation associations shows no significant improvement, suggesting that the method captures corpus-specific co-occurrences rather than transferable patterns. Ablation studies support this interpretation: training on semantically similar but non-associated passage pairs degrades retrieval below the baseline, while shuffling association pairs causes severe degradation. A downstream QA evaluation shows retrieval gains translate to +6.4 exact match improvement. The method adds 3.7ms per query, trains in under two minutes on a single GPU, and requires no LLM-based indexing.

</details>


### [63] [Robust Test-time Video-Text Retrieval: Benchmarking and Adapting for Query Shifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20851)
*Bingqing Zhang,Zhuo Cao,Heming Du,Yang Li,Xue Li,Jiajun Liu,Sen Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文针对视频文本检索模型在现实世界查询分布偏移下的脆弱性问题，构建了包含12种扰动的评估基准，揭示了查询偏移会加剧hubness现象，并提出HAT-VTR测试时适应框架，通过Hubness抑制记忆和多粒度损失显著提升了模型鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代视频文本检索模型在分布内基准测试中表现优异，但在面对现实世界查询分布偏移时会出现严重性能下降。现有图像鲁棒性解决方案无法有效处理视频的时空动态特性，缺乏针对视频查询偏移的系统性评估和专用优化方法。

Method: 1) 构建包含12种视频扰动类型和5个严重程度的综合评估基准；2) 提出HAT-VTR测试时适应框架，包含Hubness抑制记忆模块（用于优化相似度分数）和多粒度损失函数（用于强制时间特征一致性）两大核心组件。

Result: 在提出的基准测试上，HAT-VTR在多种查询偏移场景下均显著优于先前方法，大幅提升了模型在分布偏移情况下的检索性能，增强了视频文本检索系统的可靠性。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了查询分布偏移会加剧hubness现象（少数画廊项目成为主导性"中心"），而提出的HAT-VTR框架有效缓解了此问题，为视频文本检索模型在现实世界应用中的鲁棒性提供了重要保障，展现了测试时适应方法在视频领域的重要潜力。

Abstract: Modern video-text retrieval (VTR) models excel on in-distribution benchmarks but are highly vulnerable to real-world query shifts, where the distribution of query data deviates from the training domain, leading to a sharp performance drop. Existing image-focused robustness solutions are inadequate to handle this vulnerability in video, as they fail to address the complex spatio-temporal dynamics inherent in these shifts. To systematically evaluate this vulnerability, we first introduce a comprehensive benchmark featuring 12 distinct types of video perturbations across five severity degrees. Analysis on this benchmark reveals that query shifts amplify the hubness phenomenon, where a few gallery items become dominant "hubs" that attract a disproportionate number of queries. To mitigate this, we then propose HAT-VTR (Hubness Alleviation for Test-time Video-Text Retrieval), as our baseline test-time adaptation framework designed to directly counteract hubness in VTR. It leverages two key components: a Hubness Suppression Memory to refine similarity scores, and multi-granular losses to enforce temporal feature consistency. Extensive experiments demonstrate that HAT-VTR substantially improves robustness, consistently outperforming prior methods across diverse query shift scenarios, and enhancing model reliability for real-world applications.

In this work, we provide such guidance through an empirical study of how retrieval pipeline design choices affect performance and efficiency at scale.
  In particular, we examine retrieval over a variety of existing, public biomedical text datasets, leveraging a variety of disparate types of queries, including exam-style questions, conversational medical queries, community-asked questions, and non-question formulations across various retrieval pipeline settings spanning corpus selection, chunk granularity, and vector index configuration. Retrieval results are judged using a robust, win-rate comparison assessment via an LLM-as-a-judge setting with human validation.
  Across these experiments, we identify several points of concrete guidance for reviewers, including the superiority of corpus aggregation for absolute retrieval quality, and the emergence of MedRAG/pubmed as the Pareto-optimal singleton corpus under graph-based (HNSW) indexing, appropriate chunking strategies, and FAISS indexing choices that offer the best trade-offs in speed and efficiency.

### [65] [ERA: Evidence-based Reliability Alignment for Honest Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20854)
*Sunguk Shin,Meeyoung Cha,Byung-Jun Lee,Sungwon Park*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出证据可靠性对齐（ERA）框架，通过将置信度估计从标量概率扩展为显式证据分布，增强检索增强生成（RAG）系统中的拒绝回答行为。该框架利用Dirichlet分布对内外知识进行信念质量建模，并采用Dempster-Shafer理论度量知识冲突，有效区分认知与偶然不确定性，在基准测试和泛化数据集上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检索增强生成（RAG）虽能基于外部事实证据生成回答，但面临内部参数化知识与外部检索信息之间的知识冲突挑战。现有可靠性方法依赖标量置信度，无法明确区分此类混合场景中的认知不确定性（对知识的缺乏）与数据固有模糊性（偶然不确定性），导致系统无法可靠地拒绝回答不确定的问题。

Method: 提出ERA框架，包含两大核心组件：（1）情境证据量化，通过Dirichlet分布将内部模型知识与外部检索信息建模为独立信念质量；（2）知识冲突量化，运用Dempster-Shafer理论严格计算信息源间的几何不一致性。该方法可解耦认知不确定性与偶然不确定性，并根据检测到的冲突动态调节优化目标。

Result: 在标准基准和自建泛化数据集上的实验表明，ERA方法显著超越基线模型，在答案覆盖率与拒绝率之间实现更优权衡，同时具备卓越的校准性能。

Conclusion: ERA框架通过将置信度建模从标量概率转向显式证据分布，有效处理RAG系统中的知识冲突问题，成功区分认知不确定性与偶然不确定性，为提升系统可靠性和拒绝回答行为提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) grounds language models in factual evidence but introduces critical challenges regarding knowledge conflicts between internalized parameters and retrieved information. However, existing reliability methods, typically relying on scalar confidence, fail to explicitly distinguish between epistemic uncertainty and inherent data ambiguity in such hybrid scenarios. In this paper, we propose a new framework called ERA (Evidence-based Reliability Alignment) to enhance abstention behavior in RAG systems by shifting confidence estimation from scalar probabilities to explicit evidence distributions. Our method consists of two main components: (1) Contextual Evidence Quantification, which models internal and external knowledge as independent belief masses via the Dirichlet distribution, and (2) Quantifying Knowledge Conflict, which leverages Dempster-Shafer Theory (DST) to rigorously measure the geometric discordance between information sources. These components are used to disentangle epistemic uncertainty from aleatoric uncertainty and modulate the optimization objective based on detected conflicts. Experiments on standard benchmarks and a curated generalization dataset demonstrate that our approach significantly outperforms baselines, optimizing the trade-off between answer coverage and abstention with superior calibration.

</details>


### [66] [CRED-1: An Open Multi-Signal Domain Credibility Dataset for Automated Pre-Bunking of Online Misinformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20856)
*Alexander Loth,Martin Kappes,Marc-Oliver Pahl*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: CRED-1是一个开放、可复现的域名级可信度数据集，整合两个开源列表并计算四个增强信号，覆盖2672个域名，为隐私保护的浏览器扩展提供客户端虚假信息预警能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对虚假信息传播，现有数据集难以支持隐私保护的端上部署。该研究旨在构建一个可复现、开放授权且包含多维度信号的数据集，以支持在内容分发阶段进行客户端预辟谣，解决隐私保护与实时性需求。

Method: 融合OpenSources.co和Iffy.news两个开源域名列表，通过WHOIS/RDAP计算域名年龄、Tranco Top-1M评估网站流行度、Google事实核查工具API统计核查频率、Google安全浏览API检测威胁情报，最终生成0.0-1.0的综合可信度分数。整个管道仅使用Python标准库实现，确保完全可复现性。

Result: 构建了包含2672个域名的CRED-1数据集，涵盖虚假、不可靠、混合、阴谋论和讽刺五类，每个域名均配有综合可信度评分。数据集采用CC BY 4.0协议在Zenodo存档，配套代码完全开源。

Conclusion: CRED-1为隐私保护的浏览器扩展提供了端上虚假信息预辟谣的数据基础，其开放性和可复现性将促进misinformation检测领域的研究与应用发展，实现内容分发阶段的实时干预。

Abstract: This article presents CRED-1, an open, reproducible domain-level credibility dataset combining two openly-licensed source lists (OpenSources.co and Iffy.news) with four computed enrichment signals: domain age (WHOIS/RDAP), web popularity (Tranco Top-1M), fact-check frequency (Google Fact Check Tools API), and threat intelligence (Google Safe Browsing API). The dataset covers 2,672 domains categorized as fake, unreliable, mixed, conspiracy, or satire, each assigned a composite credibility score between 0.0 and 1.0. CRED-1 is designed for on-device deployment in privacy-preserving browser extensions to enable client-side pre-bunking of misinformation at the content delivery stage. The entire pipeline is implemented in Python using only standard library modules and is fully reproducible from publicly available sources. The dataset and pipeline code are released under CC~BY~4.0 and archived on Zenodo.

</details>

Existing AI scientist systems usually omit this component or fall back to an inferior alternative. To bridge this gap, we present DiagramBank, a large-scale dataset consisting of 89,422 schematic diagrams curated from existing top-tier scientific publications, designed for multimodal retrieval and exemplar-driven scientific figure generation. DiagramBank is developed through our automated curation pipeline that extracts figures and corresponding in-text references, and uses a CLIP-based filter to differentiate schematic diagrams from standard plots or natural images. Each instance is paired with rich context from abstract, caption, to figure-reference pairs, enabling information retrieval under different query granularities. We release DiagramBank in a ready-to-index format and provide a retrieval-augmented generation codebase to demonstrate exemplar-conditioned synthesis of teaser figures. DiagramBank is publicly available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/zhangt20/DiagramBank with code at https://github.com/csml-rpi/DiagramBank.

### [69] [RealRoute: Dynamic Query Routing System via Retrieve-then-Verify Paradigm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20860)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管RAG在利用外部知识 grounding LLM 方面很成功，但在处理异构数据源（如私有数据库、全局语料库和API）时仍面临挑战。现有LLM-as-a-Router方法过度依赖数据源的语义含义，当源边界模糊时容易导致路由错误。

Method: 提出RealRoute系统，将范式从预测路由转向Retrieve-then-Verify机制：采用并行、源无关的检索确保证据完整性，然后通过动态验证器交叉检查结果并合成事实依据的答案。系统支持实时可视化重新路由过程和跨知识孤岛验证链的审查。

Result: 在多跳RAG推理任务中，RealRoute显著优于预测基线方法。

Conclusion: RealRoute系统通过验证机制有效解决了多源RAG中的路由错误问题，已作为开源工具包发布并配有用户友好的Web界面。

Abstract: Despite the success of Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) in grounding LLMs with external knowledge, its application over heterogeneous sources (e.g., private databases, global corpora, and APIs) remains a significant challenge. Existing approaches typically employ an LLM-as-a-Router to dispatch decomposed sub-queries to specific sources in a predictive manner. However, this "LLM-as-a-Router" strategy relies heavily on the semantic meaning of different data sources, often leading to routing errors when source boundaries are ambiguous. In this work, we introduce RealRoute System, a framework that shifts the paradigm from predictive routing to a robust Retrieve-then-Verify mechanism. RealRoute ensures \textit{evidence completeness through parallel, source-agnostic retrieval, followed by a dynamic verifier that cross-checks the results and synthesizes a factually grounded answer}. Our demonstration allows users to visualize the real-time "re-routing" process and inspect the verification chain across multiple knowledge silos. Experiments show that RealRoute significantly outperforms predictive baselines in the multi-hop Rag reasoning task. The RealRoute system is released as an open-source toolkit with a user-friendly web interface. The code is available at the URL: https://github.com/Joseph1951210/RealRoute.

### [70] [Deep Interest Mining with Cross-Modal Alignment for SemanticID Generation in Generative Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20861)
*Yagchen Zeng*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文针对生成式推荐中语义ID(SID)存在的信息退化、语义退化和模态失真三大问题，提出集成深度情境兴趣挖掘(DCIM)、跨模态语义对齐(CMSA)和质量感知强化机制(QARM)的新框架，通过视觉-语言模型统一模态空间、重构监督保留上下文信息、强化学习筛选高质量SID，在多项基准测试中性能显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出三创新集成框架：1) 利用视觉-语言模型将非文本模态对齐至统一文本语义空间，缓解模态失真；2) 设计深度兴趣挖掘机制，通过重构监督捕获广告上下文中的隐含高级语义信息，鼓励SID保留关键情境信息；3) 构建基于质量感知奖励的强化学习框架，在后验阶段促进语义丰富的SID生成并抑制低质量SID。

Result: 大量实验表明，该方法在多个基准测试上持续优于最先进的SID生成方法，性能显著提升。消融研究进一步验证了DCIM、CMSA和QARM各组件的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过联合优化模态对齐、深度情境理解和质量感知筛选，该框架有效解决了生成式推荐中SID的多重退化问题，为大规模多模态推荐提供了新思路，推动了生成式推荐技术的发展。

Abstract: Generative Recommendation (GR) has demonstrated remarkable performance in next-token prediction paradigms, which relies on Semantic IDs (SIDs) to compress trillion-scale data into learnable vocabulary sequences. However, existing methods suffer from three critical limitations: (1) Information Degradation: the two-stage compression pipeline causes semantic loss and information degradation, with no posterior mechanism to distinguish high-quality from low-quality SIDs; (2) Semantic Degradation: cascaded quantization discards key semantic information from original multimodal features, as the embedding generation and quantization stages are not jointly optimized toward a unified objective; (3) Modality Distortion: quantizers fail to properly align text and image modalities, causing feature misalignment even when upstream networks have aligned them. To address these challenges, we propose a novel framework integrating three key innovations: Deep Contextual Interest Mining (DCIM), Cross-Modal Semantic Alignment (CMSA), and Quality-Aware Reinforcement Mechanism (QARM). First, we leverage Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to align non-textual modalities into a unified text-based semantic space, mitigating modality distortion. Second, we introduce a deep interest mining mechanism that captures high-level semantic information implicitly present in advertising contexts, encouraging SIDs to preserve critical contextual information through reconstruction-based supervision. Third, we employ a reinforcement learning framework with quality-aware rewards to encourage semantically rich SIDs while suppressing low-quality ones in the posterior stage. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach consistently outperforms state-of-the-art SID generation methods, achieving superior performance on multiple benchmarks. Ablation studies further validate the effectiveness of each proposed component

### [71] [Following the Eye-Tracking Evidence: Established Web-Search Assumptions Fail in Carousel Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21019)
*Jingwei Kang,Maarten de Rijke,Harrie Oosterhuis*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该研究通过眼动追踪实验分析了轮播界面用户行为，发现传统网页搜索的F型浏览模式和检查假设在轮播界面中不成立，提出了独特的L型浏览模式，表明现有评估指标和点击模型需要重新评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轮播界面已成为流媒体服务的标准交互形式超过十年，但对其用户行为的研究严重不足。由于缺乏实证研究，先前工作错误地假设单列表网页搜索界面的行为模式（如F型模式和检查假设）同样适用于轮播界面，这种假设是否成立亟待验证。

Method: 研究团队分析了一个新发布的眼动追踪数据集，该数据集记录了用户在轮播界面中的交互行为和检查行为，通过条件概率分析和模式识别来验证传统假设在轮播环境中的适用性。

Result: 研究发现：(i) F型模式仅适用于垂直浏览，不适用于水平滑动，且在点击条件下存在特有的L型浏览模式；(ii) 基于检查的点击率表明著名的检查假设在轮播界面中不成立；(iii) 与先前假设相反，用户普遍忽略轮播标题，直接关注内容项目。

Conclusion: 许多用户行为假设，特别是关于检查模式的假设，无法从网页搜索界面迁移到轮播推荐场景。该领域缺乏构建用户行为模型的可靠基础，因此有必要重新评估现有的轮播界面评估和点击模型。

Abstract: Carousel interfaces have been the de-facto standard for streaming media services for over a decade. Yet, there has been very little research into user behavior with such interfaces, which thus remains poorly understood. Due to this lack of empirical research, previous work has assumed that behaviors established in single-list web-search interfaces, such as the F-pattern and the examination hypothesis, also apply to carousel interfaces, for instance when designing click models or evaluation metrics. We analyze a recently-released interaction and examination dataset resulting from an eye-tracking study performed on carousel interfaces to verify whether these assumptions actually hold.
  We find that (i)~the F-pattern holds only for vertical examination and not for horizontal swiping; additionally, we discover that, when conditioned on a click, user examination follows an L-pattern unique to carousel interfaces; (ii)~click-through-rates conditioned on examination indicate that the well-known examination hypothesis does not hold in carousel interfaces; and (iii)~contrary to the assumptions of previous work, users generally ignore carousel headings and focus directly on the content items. Our findings show that many user behavior assumptions, especially concerning examination patterns, do not transfer from web search interfaces to carousel recommendation settings. Our work shows that the field lacks a reliable foundation on which to build models of user behavior with these interfaces. Consequently, a re-evaluation of existing metrics and click models for carousel interfaces may be warranted.

This makes tables one of the crucial components and information elements of scientific or regulatory documents as they are commonly utilized to present quantitative information. Extracting data from tables is typically a labor-intensive process, and alternative automated machine learning models may struggle to accurately detect and extract the relevant data due to the complex nature and diverse layouts of tabular data. The difficulty of information extraction and reading order detection is largely dependent on the structural complexity of the tables. Efforts to understand tables should prioritize capturing the content of table cells in a manner that aligns with how a human reader naturally comprehends the information. The accuracy of this task has become increasingly challenging, as manual extraction is tedious and prone to errors, especially given the staffing shortages we are currently facing. Motivation: 现有ToT检索基准主要聚焦于英语，限制了其在多语言信息访问场景中的适用性，亟需构建跨语言的评估和研究方向。

Method: 采用基于大语言模型的查询模拟框架，系统性地探究不同提示语言与源文档语言组合对合成ToT查询质量的影响，并通过与真实用户查询的系统排名相关性分析来验证模拟查询的有效性。

Result: 研究发现，实现高质量的ToT模拟需要语言感知的设计策略：非英语语言源文档对查询生成通常至关重要；然而当非英语源信息不足时，英文维基百科能够提供有益的补充信息。

Conclusion: 本研究发布了首个大规模多语言ToT基准，包含四种语言各5000条跨领域查询，为构建超越英语的真实ToT数据集提供了系统性的实践指导。

Abstract: Tip-of-the-Tongue (ToT) retrieval benchmarks have largely focused on English, limiting their applicability to multilingual information access. In this work, we construct multilingual ToT test collections for Chinese, Japanese, Korean, and English, using an LLM-based query simulation framework. We systematically study how prompt language and source document language affect the fidelity of simulated ToT queries, validating synthetic queries through system rank correlation against real user queries. Our results show that effective ToT simulation requires language-aware design choices: non-English language sources are generally important, while English Wikipedia can be beneficial when non-English sources provide insufficient information for query generation. Based on these findings, we release four ToT test collections with 5,000 queries per language across multiple domains. This work provides the first large-scale multilingual ToT benchmark and offers practical guidance for constructing realistic ToT datasets beyond English.

</details>


### [74] [PAPERMIND: Benchmarking Agentic Reasoning and Critique over Scientific Papers in Multimodal LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21304)
*Yanjun Zhao,Tianxin Wei,Jiaru Zou,Xuying Ning,Yuanchen Bei,Lingjie Chen,Simmi Rana,Wendy H. Yang,Hanghang Tong,Jingrui He*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出PAPERMIND基准，用于评估科研论文的综合理解和推理能力。该基准涵盖7个领域的真实论文，包含4类互补任务，可诊断性评估多模态基础、实验解释、跨源证据推理和批判性评估等认知能力。实验表明现有大模型在这些任务上存在持续性能差距，相关资源已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试通常孤立地评估科研论文理解的各项能力，难以作为一个统一的交互认知能力体系来评估。而理解科学论文需要整合文本和视觉信息的推理过程、解释实验证据、跨来源综合信息以及批判性评估科学主张，这要求一个能够评估综合推理能力的基准。

Method: 构建PAPERMIND基准，从农业、生物、化学、计算机科学、医学、物理和经济学7个领域收集真实科研论文，设计4类互补任务家族（多模态基础、实验解释、跨源证据推理和批判性评估）来操作化科研论文推理的不同认知层面，实现对综合推理能力的评估。

Result: 在开源和闭源多模态大语言模型上的大量实验显示，各任务间存在一致的性能差距，突显了综合科学推理和批判性评估方面持续存在的挑战，表明当前模型在集成化科学理解能力上仍有不足。

Conclusion: PAPERMIND能够通过多任务分析实现对综合科学推理行为的诊断性评估，这种评估难以通过孤立任务完成。该基准揭示了现有大模型在科学理解方面的局限，为未来研究提供了方向和资源。基准和数据集已在GitHub开源。

Abstract: Understanding scientific papers requires more than answering isolated questions or summarizing content. It involves an integrated reasoning process that grounds textual and visual information, interprets experimental evidence, synthesizes information across sources, and critically evaluates scientific claims. However, existing benchmarks typically assess these abilities in isolation, making it difficult to evaluate scientific paper understanding as a unified set of interacting cognitive abilities. In this work, we introduce PAPERMIND, a benchmark designed to evaluate integrated and agent-oriented scientific reasoning over research papers. PAPERMIND is constructed from real scientific papers across seven domains, including agriculture, biology, chemistry, computer science, medicine, physics, and economics. It comprises four complementary task families that collectively operationalize distinct cognitive facets of scientific paper reasoning, including multimodal grounding, experimental interpretation, cross-source evidence reasoning, and critical assessment. By analyzing model behavior across multiple tasks, PAPERMIND enables a diagnostic evaluation of integrated scientific reasoning behaviors that are difficult to assess through isolated task evaluations. Extensive experiments on both opensource and closed-source multimodal LLMs reveal consistent performance gaps across tasks, highlighting persistent challenges in integrated scientific reasoning and critique. Our benchmark and dataset are available at https:// github.com/Yanjun-Zhao/PaperMind.

### [75] [WPGRec: Wavelet Packet Guided Graph Enhanced Sequential Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21305)
*Peilin Liu,Zhiquan Ji,Gang Yan*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: WPGRec是一种统一的时频图增强序列推荐框架，通过小波包变换生成多尺度子带序列，在匹配尺度上进行图传播注入协作信息，并采用能量与谱平坦度感知的门控融合机制自适应聚合信息，在四个公开数据集上持续优于基线方法，尤其在稀疏和复杂行为数据集上表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有序列推荐方法面临三个核心问题：1）全局谱操作会将局部瞬态特征与长程依赖纠缠；2）基于滤波的小波处理方法在多尺度分解重构中存在时序错位和边界伪影；3）用户-项目交互图的协作信号通过尺度不一致的辅助模块注入，限制了时序动态与结构依赖的联合建模效果。为此需要一种能实现尺度对齐的时序-图结构统一建模框架。

Method: WPGRec采用三阶段架构：首先应用全树非抽取平稳小波包变换生成等长、平移不变的子带序列；然后在各子带上进行时域对齐的交互图传播，注入高阶协作信息；最后通过能量与谱平坦度感知的门控融合模块自适应聚合信息性子带并抑制类噪声成分，实现多分辨率时序建模与图传播的尺度匹配。

Result: 在四个公开基准数据集上的实验表明，WPGRec持续优于序列推荐和图基基线方法，尤其在数据稀疏且行为模式复杂的场景下优势显著，验证了频带一致性结构注入和自适应子带融合机制的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提WPGRec框架成功解决了现有多尺度时序建模与图结构注入的尺度失配问题，通过时频分析与图传播的有机结合，为噪声非平稳交互流中的用户兴趣演化建模提供了新思路，为稀疏复杂行为数据的序列推荐提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Sequential recommendation aims to model users' evolving interests from noisy and non-stationary interaction streams, where long-term preferences, short-term intents, and localized behavioral fluctuations may coexist across temporal scales. Existing frequency-domain methods mainly rely on either global spectral operations or filter-based wavelet processing. However, global spectral operations tend to entangle local transients with long-range dependencies, while filter-based wavelet pipelines may suffer from temporal misalignment and boundary artifacts during multi-scale decomposition and reconstruction. Moreover, collaborative signals from the user-item interaction graph are often injected through scale-inconsistent auxiliary modules, limiting the benefit of jointly modeling temporal dynamics and structural dependencies. To address these issues, we propose Wavelet Packet Guided Graph Enhanced Sequential Recommendation (WPGRec), a unified time-frequency and graph-enhanced framework that aligns multi-resolution temporal modeling with graph propagation at matching scales. WPGRec first applies a full-tree undecimated stationary wavelet packet transform to generate equal-length, shift-invariant subband sequences. It then performs subband-wise interaction-graph propagation to inject high-order collaborative information while preserving temporal alignment across resolutions. Finally, an energy- and spectral-flatness-aware gated fusion module adaptively aggregates informative subbands and suppresses noise-like components. Extensive experiments on four public benchmarks show that WPGRec consistently outperforms sequential and graph-based baselines, with particularly clear gains on sparse and behaviorally complex datasets, highlighting the effectiveness of band-consistent structure injection and adaptive subband fusion for sequential recommendation.

</details>

Method: 采用稀疏自编码器（SAE）学习语义概念的潜在空间，替代传统词汇表，构建SAE-SPLADE模型；系统研究两种概念的兼容性、训练策略，并对比分析其与SPLADE的差异。

Abstract: Learned Sparse IR models, such as SPLADE, offer an excellent efficiency-effectiveness tradeoff. To solve this limitation, we propose to replace the backbone vocabulary with a latent space of semantic concepts learned using Sparse Auto-Encoders (SAE). Throughout this paper, we study the compatibility of these 2 concepts, explore training approaches, and analyze the differences between our SAE-SPLADE model and traditional SPLADE models. ### [78] [Counterfactual Multi-task Learning for Delayed Conversion Modeling in E-commerce Sales Pre-Promotion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.21675)
*Xin Song,Kaiyuan Li,Jinxin Hu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对电商大促前用户加购不转化导致的延迟反馈与转化率低迷问题，本文提出CM-DCM模型，通过多任务联合建模直接转化与延迟转化、个性化门控缓解数据稀疏性、反事实因果推理ATC到延迟转化的转移概率，有效提升大促前CVR预测准确性与GMV表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注促销日当天的转化率预测，却忽视了大促前用户行为模式的特殊性：用户倾向于搜索浏览、加购待买，导致转化延迟且CVR显著降低。同时，传统延迟反馈模型假设延迟转化在连续时间窗口内分布，但大促场景中延迟转化高度集中于促销日，存在独特的分布偏移，现有方法无法有效建模这一现象。

Method: 提出反事实多任务延迟转化模型(CM-DCM)，包含三大创新：(1) 多任务学习框架，利用历史大促前数据联合建模直接转化与延迟转化任务；(2) 个性化用户行为门控模块，动态调整行为表示以缓解短周期预促销阶段的数据稀疏问题；(3) 基于反事实因果推断的方法，显式建模从加购到延迟转化的转移概率，捕捉用户决策的因果机制。

Result: 离线实验表明CM-DCM在预促销场景下显著优于各类基线模型。在线A/B测试在大型促销活动中验证，模型在广告收入、延迟转化GMV及整体GMV等核心业务指标上均取得显著提升，证明了其实际应用价值。

Conclusion: CM-DCM首次系统性地解决了大促前延迟转化预测的分布偏移与数据稀疏挑战，通过因果推理与多任务学习的有机结合，为电商平台在预热期精准识别潜在转化用户提供了有效方案，具备较强的业务落地能力。

Abstract: Sales promotions, as short-term incentives to stimulate product purchases, play a pivotal role in modern e-commerce marketing strategies. During promotional events, user behavior patterns exhibit distinct characteristics compared to regular periods. In the pre-promotion phase, users typically engage in product search and browsing without immediate purchases, adding items to carts in anticipation of promotional discounts. This behavior leads to delayed conversions, resulting in significantly lower conversion rates (CVR) before the promotion day. Although existing research has made progress in CVR prediction for promotion days using historical data, it largely overlooks the critical pre-promotion period. And delayed feedback modeling has been extensively studied, current approaches fail to account for the unique distribution shifts in conversion behavior before promotional events, where delayed conversions predominantly occur on the promotion day rather than over continuous time windows. To address these limitations, we propose the Counterfactual Multi-task Delayed Conversion Model (CM-DCM), which leverages historical pre-promotion data to enhance CVR prediction for both delayed and direct conversions. Our model incorporates three key innovations: (i) A multi-task architecture that jointly models direct and delayed conversions using historical pre-promotion data; (ii) A personalized user behavior gating module to mitigate data sparsity issues during brief pre-promotion periods; (iii) A counterfactual causal approach to model the transition probability from add-to-cart (ATC) to delayed conversion. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CM-DCM outperforms baselines in pre-promotion scenarios. Online A/B tests during major promotional events showed significant improvements in advertising revenue, delayed conversion GMV, and overall GMV, validating the effectiveness of our approach.

*Anas Buhayh,Elizabeth McKinnie,Clement Canel,Robin Burke*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过理论分析与模拟实验，考察用户在切换算法时数据可移植性机制对用户模型重建的影响，并评估不同推荐算法在此过程中的效用变化。

Result: 研究发现数据可移植性对不同推荐算法的用户效用产生差异化影响：部分算法在数据迁移后表现提升，而另一些则出现性能下降，表明数据可移植性的效果具有算法依赖性。

Abstract: Optimizing outcomes for multiple stakeholders in recommender systems has historically focused on algorithmic interventions, such as developing multi-objective models or re-ranking results from existing algorithms. However, structural changes to the recommendation ecosystem itself remain understudied. This paper explores the implications of algorithmic pluralism (also known as "middleware" in the governance literature), in which recommendation algorithms are decoupled from platforms, enabling users to select their preferred algorithm. Prior simulation work demonstrates that algorithmic choice benefits niche consumers and providers. Yet this approach raises critical questions about user modeling in the context of data portability: when users switch algorithms, what happens to their data? Noting that multiple data portability regulations have emerged to strengthen user data ownership and control. We examine how such policies affect user models and stakeholders' outcomes in recommendation setting. Our findings reveal that data portability scenarios produce varying effects on user utility across different recommendation algorithms. We highlight key policy considerations and implications for designing equitable recommendation ecosystems.

### [80] [CaST-POI: Candidate-Conditioned Spatiotemporal Modeling for Next POI Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20845)
*Zhenyu Yu,Chunlei Meng,Yangchen Zeng,Mohd Yamani Idna Idris,Shuigeng Zhou*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: CaST-POI是一种候选条件化的时空模型，用于下一个兴趣点推荐。该模型通过候选点作为查询动态解读用户历史轨迹，并引入候选相对时空偏置，在三个基准数据集上显著优于现有方法，特别在大候选池场景下优势明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法采用候选无关范式，从历史轨迹计算单一用户表示并统一评分所有候选POI，忽略了历史访问的相关性实际上取决于正在评估的具体候选点。这种静态用户表示无法针对不同候选点动态调整理解，导致推荐精度受限。

Method: 提出CaST-POI模型：1）候选条件化序列读取器，将候选点作为查询向量，通过注意力机制动态选择与当前候选相关的历史轨迹片段；2）候选相对时空偏置模块，建模历史访问与各候选点之间的细粒度时空关系，捕捉个性化移动模式。

Result: 在三个基准数据集上的广泛实验表明，CaST-POI在所有评估指标上持续优于当前最优方法，提升幅度显著。特别值得注意的是，当候选池规模较大时，模型性能优势更加突出，证明了候选条件化策略的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究验证了"相同的用户历史应基于不同候选点差异化解读"的核心思想，候选条件化范式为移动性推荐提供了新视角。通过动态注意力机制和相对时空偏置的协同作用，显著提升了下一POI推荐性能，尤其在候选空间扩展时更具鲁棒性。

Abstract: Next Point-of-Interest (POI) recommendation plays a crucial role in location-based services by predicting users' future mobility patterns. Existing methods typically compute a single user representation from historical trajectories and use it to score all candidate POIs uniformly. However, this candidate-agnostic paradigm overlooks that the relevance of historical visits inherently depends on which candidate is being evaluated. In this paper, we propose CaST-POI, a candidate-conditioned spatiotemporal model for next POI recommendation. Our key insight is that the same user history should be interpreted differently when evaluating different candidate POIs. CaST-POI employs a candidate-conditioned sequence reader that uses candidates as queries to dynamically attend to user history. In addition, we introduce candidate-relative temporal and spatial biases to capture fine-grained mobility patterns based on the relationships between historical visits and each candidate POI. Extensive experiments on three benchmark datasets demonstrate that CaST-POI consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods, yielding substantial improvements across multiple evaluation metrics, with particularly strong advantages under large candidate pools. Code is available at https://github.com/YuZhenyuLindy/CaST-POI.git.

</details>

### [81] [Frequency-Forcing: From Scaling-as-Time to Soft Frequency Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20902)
*Weitao Du*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出Frequency-Forcing，一种基于"forcing"软约束机制的尺度有序生成方法。通过轻量可学习的小波包变换从数据自身提取低频辅助流，以异步时间调度引导标准像素流早期生成低频结构，在避免硬频率约束坐标重写和外部依赖的同时，实现了K-Flow的频率排序效果，并在ImageNet-256上取得SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准流匹配模型均匀输运噪声到数据，但自然图像合成需要从粗到细的生成顺序（先低频结构后高频细节）。现有方法存在局限：K-Flow采用硬频率约束但需重写核心流坐标，Latent Forcing虽使用软约束机制却依赖外部预训练编码器（如DINO）。亟需一种既能保持软约束优势，又能自适应学习数据相关频率基的路径保持型方法。

Method: 提出Frequency-Forcing，核心是"self-forcing"机制：1) **频率scratchpad构建**：使用轻量可学习的小波包变换直接从数据学习频率基，替代外部预训练编码器；2) **异步时间调度**：设计低频辅助流比像素流更早成熟的耦合机制；3) **软约束引导**：在标准像素流匹配框架中，通过forcing项引导早期生成低频成分，实现K-Flow的频率排序效果但不改变核心流坐标。该方法避免了外部依赖，学习的频率基更适应数据统计特性。

Result: 在ImageNet-256数据集上，Frequency-Forcing相比强像素空间和隐空间基线持续提升FID指标，验证了其有效性。更重要的是，该方法能自然地与语义流组合，产生进一步的协同增益，证明了其良好的可扩展性和通用性。

Conclusion: Forcing-based尺度排序是一种通用、路径保持的替代方案，相比硬频率流方法更灵活。它通过数据驱动的自适应频率基学习和软约束机制，为生成模型提供了新的设计范式，在保持核心流结构的同时实现了有效的多尺度生成控制。

Abstract: While standard flow-matching models transport noise to data uniformly, incorporating an explicit generation order - specifically, establishing coarse, low-frequency structure before fine detail - has proven highly effective for synthesizing natural images. Two recent works offer distinct paradigms for this. K-Flow imposes a hard frequency constraint by reinterpreting a frequency scaling variable as flow time, running the trajectory inside a transformed amplitude space. Latent Forcing provides a soft ordering mechanism by coupling the pixel flow with an auxiliary semantic latent flow via asynchronous time schedules, leaving the pixel interpolation path itself untouched. Viewed from the angle of improving pixel generation, we observe that forcing - guiding generation with an earlier-maturing auxiliary stream - offers a highly compatible route to scale-ordered generation without rewriting the core flow coordinate. Building on this, we propose Frequency-Forcing, which realizes K-Flow's frequency ordering through Latent Forcing's soft mechanism: a standard pixel flow is guided by an auxiliary low-frequency stream that matures earlier in time. Unlike Latent Forcing, whose scratchpad relies on a heavy pretrained encoder (e.g., DINO), our frequency scratchpad is derived from the data itself via a lightweight learnable wavelet packet transform. We term this a self-forcing signal, which avoids external dependencies while learning a basis better adapted to data statistics than the fixed bases used in hard frequency flows. On ImageNet-256, Frequency-Forcing consistently improves FID over strong pixel- and latent-space baselines, and naturally composes with a semantic stream to yield further gains. This illustrates that forcing-based scale ordering is a versatile, path-preserving alternative to hard frequency flows.

</details>


### [82] [Do Masked Autoencoders Improve Downhole Prediction? An Empirical Study on Real Well Drilling Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20909)
*Aleksander Berezowski,Hassan Hassanzadeh,Gouri Ginde*

TL;DR: 针对井下钻井数据标签稀缺问题，本研究首次评估了掩码自编码器预训练方法，在350万步数据上发现最佳配置比GRU基线降低19.8%的MAE，揭示了潜在空间宽度是主导因素而掩码比例影响微弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 井下钻井遥测存在根本性标注不对称：地面传感器数据以1Hz连续生成，而井下测量成本高、间歇且稀缺。现有机器学习方法普遍采用从零开始的全监督训练，难以适应这种数据模式。

Method: 首次对掩码自编码器(MAE)预训练进行实证评估。使用两个公开的犹他州FORGE地热井数据（约350万时间步），通过72种MAE配置的全因子设计空间搜索，并与监督式LSTM和GRU基线比较，任务为预测总泥浆体积。

Result: 最佳MAE配置使测试MAE相对GRU基线降低19.8%，但比LSTM基线高6.4%。分析发现潜在空间宽度是主导架构选择（与测试MAE的Pearson r=-0.59），而掩码比例影响可忽略，这归因于1Hz钻井数据的高时间冗余性。

Conclusion: MAE预训练为钻井分析建立了可行范式，并明确了其最有利的应用条件。

Abstract: Downhole drilling telemetry presents a fundamental labeling asymmetry: surface sensor data are generated continuously at 1~Hz, while labeled downhole measurements are costly, intermittent, and scarce. Current machine learning approaches for downhole metric prediction universally adopt fully supervised training from scratch, which is poorly suited to this data regime. We present the first empirical evaluation of masked autoencoder (MAE) pretraining for downhole drilling metric prediction. Using two publicly available Utah FORGE geothermal wells comprising approximately 3.5 million timesteps of multivariate drilling telemetry, we conduct a systematic full-factorial design space search across 72 MAE configurations and compare them against supervised LSTM and GRU baselines on the task of predicting Total Mud Volume. Results show that the best MAE configuration reduces test mean absolute error by 19.8\% relative to the supervised GRU baseline, while trailing the supervised LSTM baseline by 6.4\%. Analysis of design dimensions reveals that latent space width is the dominant architectural choice (Pearson $r = -0.59$ with test MAE), while masking ratio has negligible effect, an unexpected finding attributed to high temporal redundancy in 1~Hz drilling data. These results establish MAE pretraining as a viable paradigm for drilling analytics and identify the conditions under which it is most beneficial.

### [83] [FairyFuse: Multiplication-Free LLM Inference on CPUs via Fused Ternary Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20913)
*Fei Zuo,Xiaoyan Xi,Quanyi Zeng,Feiyu Wang,Ho Fai Leung*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FairyFuse是一个针对CPU平台的乘法免费推理系统，通过将8个子GEMV融合到单个AVX-512循环中使用掩码加减运算，在内存受限的CPU上实现29.6倍的内核加速和32.4 tokens/s的端到端性能，比llama.cpp Q4_K_M快1.24倍且质量几乎无损。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在仅CPU平台上，大语言模型的内存带宽是主要瓶颈。现有系统即使对权重进行4位量化，仍需反量化并执行浮点乘法，限制了性能提升。虽然三值权重（-1,0,+1）可用条件加减代替乘法，但现有运行时未充分利用此结构。

Method: 将每个广泛线性层的8个实值子GEMV融合到单个AVX-512循环中，通过掩码加法和减法实现乘法免费执行。

Result: 在Intel Xeon 8558P上实现32.4 tokens/s，比llama.cpp Q4_K_M快1.24倍。WikiText-2困惑度5.52 vs FP16的5.47，下游准确率66.0%。Roofline分析显示16x压缩使GEMV从内存受限转向计算受限，在带宽受限CPU上实现29.6x内核加速，但在GPU上收益甚微。

Conclusion: FairyFure通过利用三值权重结构和AVX-512指令集，在CPU平台上实现了高效的乘法免费推理，在保持几乎无损质量的同时显著提升性能，特别适合内存带宽受限的CPU环境。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed on CPU-only platforms where memory bandwidth is the primary bottleneck for autoregressive generation. Weight quantization to four bits or below reduces memory pressure, yet existing systems still dequantize weights and perform floating-point multiplications, limiting the achievable gains. Ternary weights in {-1, 0, +1} provide a more efficient alternative, replacing multiplications with conditional additions, subtractions, or no-ops. While Fairy2i shows that ternary LLMs can match FP16 quality, its runtime does not exploit this structure. We present FairyFuse, an inference system that enables multiplication-free execution on commodity CPUs by fusing the eight real-valued sub-GEMVs of each widely-linear layer into a single AVX-512 loop using masked additions and subtractions, with zero floating-point multiplications. Roofline analysis shows that 16x weight compression shifts memory-bound GEMV toward the compute regime on bandwidth-limited CPUs, yielding a 29.6x kernel speedup while offering little benefit on GPUs. End-to-end, FairyFuse achieves 32.4 tokens per second on a single Intel Xeon 8558P, outperforming llama.cpp Q4_K_M by 1.24x with near-lossless quality (WikiText-2 perplexity 5.52 vs. 5.47 FP16; downstream accuracy 66.0%).

*Yuzhen Mao,Michael Y. Li,Emily B. Fox*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Gist Sparse Attention (GSA)，一种可学习的压缩方法，通过gist token作为稀疏注意力的路由信号，无需修改架构即可实现长上下文高效处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型扩展到长上下文面临全注意力二次计算成本挑战。现有缓解方法如KV-cache选择或压缩技术存在局限，需要无需架构修改的端到端可学习解决方案。

Method: 提出基于GSA的选择性展开方法：将上下文压缩为可学习的gist token，选择最相关gist，再恢复对应原始块进行细粒度注意力；通过递归的gist-of-gist构建实现多分辨率上下文访问，解码复杂度为对数级；整个过程以端到端方式纳入训练。

Result: 在LongBench和RAG基准测试上，该方法在8×至32×压缩率范围内，持续优于其他压缩基线和推理时稀疏注意力方法。

Conclusion: GSA通过结合紧凑全局表示与目标细粒度证据的粗到细机制，为扩展LLM到长上下文提供了有效的端到端可学习解决方案，实证表现优异。

Abstract: Scaling large language models to long contexts is challenging due to the quadratic computational cost of full attention. Mitigation approaches include KV-cache selection or compression techniques. We instead provide an effective and end-to-end learnable bridge between the two without requiring architecture modification. In particular, our key insight is that interleaved gist compression tokens -- which provide a learnable summary of sets of raw tokens -- can serve as routing signals for sparse attention. Building on this, we introduce selective unfolding via GSA, which first compresses the context into gist tokens, then selects the most relevant gists, and subsequently restores the corresponding raw chunks for detailed attention. This yields a simple coarse-to-fine mechanism that combines compact global representations with targeted access to fine-grained evidence. We further incorporate this process directly into training in an end-to-end fashion, avoiding the need for external retrieval modules. In addition, we extend the framework hierarchically via recursive gist-of-gist construction, enabling multi-resolution context access with logarithmic per-step decoding complexity. Empirical results on LongBench and RAG benchmarks demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms other compression baselines as well as inference-time sparse attention methods across compression ratios from $8\times$ to $32\times$. The code is available at: https://github.com/yuzhenmao/gist-sparse-attention/

### [86] [ILDR: Geometric Early Detection of Grokking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20923)
*Shreel Golwala*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Inter/Intra-class Distance Ratio (ILDR)作为grokking的早期检测指标，该几何度量基于倒数第二层表征空间，能在验证准确率跃升前9-73%的训练周期检测到转变，且具有跨随机种子的稳定性，可作为早停触发器并实现双向控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有grokking检测信号存在根本缺陷：权重范数反映参数正则化但滞后于转变；GrokFast的慢梯度EMA在不同随机种子间极不稳定（标准差超过平均提前时间）。亟需一种直接、稳定且对记忆化鲁棒的早期检测指标。

Method: 提出ILDR：计算倒数第二层表征的类间质心分离度与类内离散度之比，基于Fisher线性判别准则，无需特征分解，复杂度O(|C|²+N)。该度量仅使用验证集数据，避免记忆化效应，通过几何重排信号预测泛化跃迁。

Result: ILDR在转变前升至基线2.5倍；在8个种子上平均提前950±250步（变异系数26%）；转变后表征方差骤降1696倍；作为早停触发器减少18.6%训练开销；在阈值处进行优化器干预可实现转变的双向控制，表明其跟踪的是泛化的表征条件而非下游相关现象。

Conclusion: ILDR提供了grokking的几何指纹，直接捕捉表征空间的相变前兆，而非间接相关信号。其稳定性、可解释性和可操作性使其成为理解和控制系统性泛化现象的有效工具。

Abstract: Grokking describes a delayed generalization phenomenon in which a neural network achieves perfect training accuracy long before validation accuracy improves, followed by an abrupt transition to strong generalization. Existing detection signals are indirect: weight norm reflects parameter-space regularization and consistently lags the transition, while GrokFast's slow gradient EMA, used without gradient amplification, is unstable across seeds with standard deviation exceeding mean lead time. We propose the Inter/Intra-class Distance Ratio (ILDR), a geometric metric computed on second-to-last layer representations as the ratio of inter-class centroid separation to intra-class scatter. ILDR provides an early detection signal: it rises and crosses a threshold at 2.5 times its baseline before the grokking transition appears in validation accuracy, indicating early geometric reorganization in representation space. Grounded in Fisher's linear discriminant criterion, ILDR requires no eigendecomposition and runs in O(|C|^2 + N). It is evaluated exclusively on held-out data, making it robust to memorization effects. Across modular arithmetic and permutation group composition (S5), ILDR leads the grokking transition by 9 to 73 percent of the training budget, with lead time increasing with task algebraic complexity. Over eight random seeds, ILDR leads by 950 +/- 250 steps with a coefficient of variation of 26 percent, and post-grokking variance drops by 1696 times, consistent with a sharp phase transition in representation space. Using ILDR as an early stopping trigger reduces training by 18.6 percent on average. Optimizer interventions triggered at the ILDR threshold demonstrate bidirectional control over the transition, suggesting ILDR tracks representational conditions underlying generalization rather than a downstream correlate.

</details>

To address this limitation, we propose a Large Language Model (LLM)-guided temporal simulation framework that explicitly models physiological trajectories prior to disease onset for clinically interpretable prediction. The framework consists of a spatiotemporal feature extraction module that captures dynamic dependencies among multivariate vital signs, a Medical Prompt-as-Prefix module that embeds clinical reasoning cues into LLMs, and an agent-based post-processing component that constrains predictions within physiologically plausible ranges. By first simulating the evolution of key physiological indicators and then classifying sepsis onset, our model offers transparent prediction mechanisms that align with clinical judgment. Evaluated on the MIMIC-IV and eICU databases, the proposed method achieves superior AUC scores (0.861-0.903) across 24-4-hour pre-onset prediction tasks, outperforming conventional deep learning and rule-based approaches. More importantly, it provides interpretable trajectories and risk trends that can assist clinicians in early intervention and personalized decision-making in intensive care environments.

### [88] [Domain-Aware Hierarchical Contrastive Learning for Semi-Supervised Generalization Fault Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20928)
*Junyu Ren,Wensheng Gan,Philip S Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对标记数据稀缺下未见工况的故障诊断难题，本文提出域感知分层对比学习（DAHCL）框架。该框架通过域感知学习模块校准跨域伪标签偏差，并通过分层对比学习结合动态置信度分层与模糊监督，提升未标记样本利用率与表示学习质量，在三个基准数据集上验证了有效性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出统一的DAHCL框架，包含两个核心模块：1）域感知学习（DAL）模块，显式捕捉源域几何特征并校准异构源域间的伪标签预测，缓解跨域偏差；2）分层对比学习（HCL）模块，融合动态置信度分层与模糊对比监督，使不确定样本无需依赖不可靠的硬标签即可参与表示学习。同时将工程噪声纳入评估协议。

Conclusion: DAHCL框架通过域感知校准与分层对比学习，为工程实践中标记数据稀缺且工况复杂的故障诊断问题提供了有效解决方案，验证了两模块在提升跨域泛化能力方面的有效性。

Abstract: Fault diagnosis under unseen operating conditions remains highly challenging when labeled data are scarce. Semi-supervised domain generalization fault diagnosis (SSDGFD) provides a practical solution by jointly exploiting labeled and unlabeled source domains. However, existing methods still suffer from two coupled limitations. First, pseudo-labels for unlabeled domains are typically generated primarily from knowledge learned on the labeled source domain, which neglects domain-specific geometric discrepancies and thus induces systematic cross-domain pseudo-label bias. Second, unlabeled samples are commonly handled with a hard accept-or-discard strategy, where rigid thresholding causes imbalanced sample utilization across domains, while hard-label assignment for uncertain samples can easily introduce additional noise. To address these issues, we propose a unified framework termed domain-aware hierarchical contrastive learning (DAHCL) for SSDGFD. Specifically, DAHCL introduces a domain-aware learning (DAL) module to explicitly capture source-domain geometric characteristics and calibrate pseudo-label predictions across heterogeneous source domains, thereby mitigating cross-domain bias in pseudo-label generation. In addition, DAHCL develops a hierarchical contrastive learning (HCL) module that combines dynamic confidence stratification with fuzzy contrastive supervision, enabling uncertain samples to contribute to representation learning without relying on unreliable hard labels. In this way, DAHCL jointly improves the quality of supervision and the utilization of unlabeled samples. Furthermore, to better reflect practical industrial scenarios, we incorporate engineering noise into the SSDGFD evaluation protocol. ### [89] [Data-Driven Open-Loop Simulation for Digital-Twin Operator Decision Support in Wastewater Treatment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20935)

Abstract: Wastewater treatment plants (WWTPs) need digital-twin-style decision support tools that can simulate plant response under prescribed control plans, tolerate irregular and missing sensing, and remain informative over 12-36 h planning horizons. ### [90] [Sink-Token-Aware Pruning for Fine-Grained Video Understanding in Efficient Video LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20937)
*Kibum Kim,Jiwan Kim,Kyle Min,Yueqi Wang,Jinyoung Moon,Julian McAuley,Chanyoung Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对视频大语言模型因视觉token过多导致的高推理延迟问题，现有无训练token剪枝方法在粗粒度MCQA任务上有效，但在需要精确视觉grounding的细粒度任务（如幻觉评估）上出现性能急剧下降。本文揭示"汇聚token"（语义无意义但吸引异常高注意力的token）是主要障碍，并提出SToP方法，通过引入汇聚分数抑制这些token，在高达90%剪枝率下仍显著提升视频理解性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频大语言模型因输入大量视觉token而产生高昂推理延迟。现有训练无关的token剪枝方法虽能降低计算成本，但仅在粗粒度的多项选择题问答基准上验证有效。对于需要精确视觉grounding的细粒度理解任务，这些方法存在性能崩溃问题，其根本原因尚未被系统分析。

Method: 提出汇聚token感知剪枝（SToP）方法。首先识别"汇聚token"——语义信息匮乏却吸引过度注意力权重的token。通过计算每个token的汇聚分数来量化其成为汇聚token的倾向，并将该分数集成到现有空间和时间剪枝策略中，在剪枝过程中主动抑制汇聚token的保留，从而减少其对视觉证据的干扰。该方法为即插即用的简单有效方案。

Result: 在VisionZip、FastVid和Holitom等先进剪枝方法上应用SToP，并在幻觉评估、开放生成、组合推理和MCQA等多种基准测试中验证。结果表明，SToP能显著提升细粒度视频理解性能，解决了现有方法在细粒度任务上的性能崩溃问题，即使剪除高达90%的视觉token仍保持良好效果。

Conclusion: 汇聚token是导致视频token剪枝方法在细粒度理解任务上失效的关键因素。SToP通过显式识别和抑制汇聚token，为视频大语言模型的高效推理提供了简单有效的即插即用解决方案，显著提升了剪枝后的模型性能，对实现低延迟视频理解具有重要意义。

Abstract: Video Large Language Models (Video LLMs) incur high inference latency due to a large number of visual tokens provided to LLMs. To address this, training-free visual token pruning has emerged as a solution to reduce computational costs; however, existing methods are primarily validated on Multiple-Choice Question Answering (MCQA) benchmarks, where coarse-grained cues often suffice. In this work, we reveal that these methods suffer a sharp performance collapse on fine-grained understanding tasks requiring precise visual grounding, such as hallucination evaluation. To explore this gap, we conduct a systematic analysis and identify sink tokens--semantically uninformative tokens that attract excessive attention--as a key obstacle to fine-grained video understanding. When these sink tokens survive pruning, they distort the model's visual evidence and hinder fine-grained understanding. Motivated by these insights, we propose Sink-Token-aware Pruning (SToP), a simple yet effective plug-and-play method that introduces a sink score to quantify each token's tendency to behave as a sink and applies this score to existing spatial and temporal pruning methods to suppress them, thereby enhancing video understanding. To validate the effectiveness of SToP, we apply it to state-of-the-art pruning methods (VisionZip, FastVid, and Holitom) and evaluate it across diverse benchmarks covering hallucination, open-ended generation, compositional reasoning, and MCQA. Our results demonstrate that SToP significantly boosts performance, even when pruning up to 90% of visual tokens.

### [91] [SCM: Sleep-Consolidated Memory with Algorithmic Forgetting for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20943)

Method: SCM借鉴神经科学原理，构建五大核心组件：1）有限容量工作记忆；2）多维重要性标记机制；3）离线睡眠阶段巩固（区分NREM与REM睡眠相）；4）意向性价值导向遗忘；5）支持内省计算的自模型。

Abstract: We present SCM (Sleep-Consolidated Memory), a research preview of a memory architecture for large language models that draws on neuroscientific principles to address a fundamental limitation in current systems: the absence of persistent, structured, and biologically plausible memory. Existing approaches rely on truncating context windows, growing vector databases without bound, or tiered storage systems that lack consolidation and forgetting mechanisms. SCM implements five core components inspired by human memory: a limited-capacity working memory, multi-dimensional importance tagging, offline sleep-stage consolidation with distinct NREM and REM phases, intentional value-based forgetting, and a computational self-model enabling introspection. We also discuss how the integration of LAF and UTTL bridges the gap between logical semantics and statistical optimization. Method: 提出两种后处理技术：1）随机选择：从一组在相同数据集上训练但具有不同隐私-效用权衡的现有模型中随机选择一个模型；2）线性组合：将多个现有模型进行线性组合以生成新模型。从Rényi差分隐私和隐私损失分布的角度为这些方法提供隐私核算。

Result: 在私有均值估计的案例研究中，完全刻画了隐私-效用结果，并从理论上证明了线性组合方法优于随机选择。在多个模型和合成/真实数据集上的实验验证了所提出方法和分析的有效性。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了通过后处理技术可以灵活地满足动态变化的隐私需求，避免了重复训练的成本，为差分隐私机器学习模型的部署提供了实用且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: In machine learning applications, privacy requirements during inference or deployment time could change constantly due to varying policies, regulations, or user experience. In this work, we aim to generate a magnitude of models to satisfy any target differential privacy (DP) requirement without additional training steps, given a set of existing models trained on the same dataset with different privacy/utility tradeoffs. We propose two post processing techniques, namely random selection and linear combination, to output a final private model for any target privacy parameter. We provide privacy accounting of these approaches from the lens of R'enyi DP and privacy loss distributions for general problems. In a case study on private mean estimation, we fully characterize the privacy/utility results and theoretically establish the superiority of linear combination over random selection. Empirically, we validate our approach and analyses on several models and both synthetic and real-world datasets.
